		<script>
			let cscoDarkMode = {};

			(function () {
				const body = document.querySelector('html[data-scheme]');

				cscoDarkMode = {
					init: function (e) {
						this.initMode(e);
						window
							.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')
							.addListener((e) => {
								this.initMode(e);
							});

						window.addEventListener('load', () => {
							document.querySelectorAll('.header__toggle-scheme').forEach(el => {
								el.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
									e.preventDefault();
									if ('auto' === body.getAttribute('data-scheme')) {
										if (
											window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches
										) {
											cscoDarkMode.changeScheme('light', true);
										} else if (
											window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches
										) {
											cscoDarkMode.changeScheme('dark', true);
										}
									} else {
										if ('dark' === body.getAttribute('data-scheme')) {
											cscoDarkMode.changeScheme('light', true);
										} else {
											cscoDarkMode.changeScheme('dark', true);
										}
									}
								});
							})
						});
					},
					initMode: function (e) {
						let siteScheme = false;
						switch (
							'light' // Field. User’s system preference.
						) {
							case 'dark':
								siteScheme = 'dark';
								break;
							case 'light':
								siteScheme = 'light';
								break;
							case 'system':
								siteScheme = 'auto';
								break;
						}
						if ('false') {
							// Field. Enable dark/light mode toggle.
							if ('light' === localStorage.getItem('_color_schema')) {
								siteScheme = 'light';
							}
							if ('dark' === localStorage.getItem('_color_schema')) {
								siteScheme = 'dark';
							}
						}
						if (siteScheme && siteScheme !== body.getAttribute('data-scheme')) {
							this.changeScheme(siteScheme, false);
						}
					},
					changeScheme: function (siteScheme, cookie) {
						body.classList.add('scheme-toggled');
						body.setAttribute('data-scheme', siteScheme);
						if (cookie) {
							localStorage.setItem('_color_schema', siteScheme);
						}
						setTimeout(() => {
							body.classList.remove('scheme-toggled');
						}, 100);
					},
				};
			})();

			cscoDarkMode.init();

			document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', function () {
				setTimeout(() => {
					cscoDarkMode.init();
				}, 100);
			});
		</script>

    <button class="clickable-banner-slider__nav clickable-banner-slider__nav--prev" onclick="if(!isAnimating) changeSlide(-1)">
      <svg class="clickable-banner-slider__nav-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
        <path d="M15.41 7.41L14 6l-6 6 6 6 1.41-1.41L10.83 12z"/>

    <button class="clickable-banner-slider__nav clickable-banner-slider__nav--next" onclick="if(!isAnimating) changeSlide(1)">
      <svg class="clickable-banner-slider__nav-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
        <path d="M10 6L8.59 7.41 13.17 12l-4.58 4.59L10 18l6-6z"/>

<script>
  let currentSlide = 0;
  let slideInterval;
  let isAnimating = false;
  const autoRotate = true;
  const slideChangeInterval = 4 * 1000;

  function initSlider() {
    const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-banner-slider__slide');
    const dots = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-banner-slider__dot');
    const slidesContainer = document.querySelector('.clickable-banner-slider__slides');
    const slider = document.querySelector('.clickable-banner-slider');
    
    // console.log('=== SLIDER INIT DEBUG ===');
    // console.log('Found slides:', slides.length);
    // console.log('Found dots:', dots.length);
    // console.log('Slides container:', slidesContainer);
    
    // Debug each slide
    slides.forEach((slide, index) => {
      // console.log(`Slide ${index}:`, {
      //   element: slide,
      //   width: slide.offsetWidth,
      //   height: slide.offsetHeight,
      //   display: getComputedStyle(slide).display,
      //   visibility: getComputedStyle(slide).visibility
      // });
    });
    
    // Debug container
    if (slidesContainer) {
      // console.log('Container debug:', {
      //   width: slidesContainer.offsetWidth,
      //   height: slidesContainer.offsetHeight,
      //   scrollWidth: slidesContainer.scrollWidth,
      //   display: getComputedStyle(slidesContainer).display,
      //   transform: getComputedStyle(slidesContainer).transform
      // });
    }
    
    if (!slidesContainer || slides.length <= 1) {
      // console.log('Not enough slides, exiting init');
      return;
    }

    // Find the first active slide (set by Liquid template)
    let foundActiveSlide = false;
    slides.forEach((slide, index) => {
      if (slide.classList.contains('active') && !foundActiveSlide) {
        currentSlide = index;
        foundActiveSlide = true;
        // console.log(`Found active slide at index: ${index}`);
      }
    });

    // If no active slide found, set the first slide as active
    if (!foundActiveSlide && slides.length > 0) {
      currentSlide = 0;
      slides[0].classList.add('active');
      slides[0].classList.remove('entering-from-right', 'exiting-to-left');
      // console.log('No active slide found, setting first slide as active');
    }

    // Ensure other slides are properly positioned
    slides.forEach((slide, index) => {
      if (index !== currentSlide) {
        slide.classList.add('entering-from-right');
        slide.classList.remove('active', 'exiting-to-left');
      }
    });

    // console.log('Slider positioning validated');

    // Update dots to match current slide
    updateDots();

    // Start auto-rotation if enabled
    if (autoRotate) {
      startAutoRotation();
    }

    // Pause auto-rotation on hover
    if (slider && autoRotate) {
      slider.addEventListener('mouseenter', stopAutoRotation);
      slider.addEventListener('mouseleave', startAutoRotation);
    }
    
    // console.log('=== SLIDER INIT COMPLETE ===');
  }

  function changeSlide(direction) {
    const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-banner-slider__slide');
    
    if (slides.length <= 1 || isAnimating) {
      // console.log('Blocked: Animation in progress or not enough slides');
      return;
    }

    const oldSlideIndex = currentSlide;

    // Calculate new slide index
    currentSlide += direction;
    if (currentSlide >= slides.length) {
      currentSlide = 0;
    } else if (currentSlide < 0) {
      currentSlide = slides.length - 1;
    }

    // console.log(`Changing from slide ${oldSlideIndex} to ${currentSlide}`);

    // Animate between slides
    animateSlideTransition(oldSlideIndex, currentSlide);

    // Update dots
    updateDots();

    // Reset auto-rotation timer
    if (autoRotate) {
      stopAutoRotation();
      // Restart after animation completes
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (autoRotate) {
          startAutoRotation();
        }
      }, 700); // Wait for animation to fully complete (650ms + buffer)
    }
  }

  function goToSlide(slideIndex) {
    const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-banner-slider__slide');
    
    if (slides.length <= 1 || slideIndex === currentSlide || isAnimating) {
      // console.log('Blocked: Animation in progress or invalid slide');
      return;
    }

    const oldSlideIndex = currentSlide;
    currentSlide = slideIndex;

    // Animate between slides
    animateSlideTransition(oldSlideIndex, currentSlide);

    // Update dots
    updateDots();

    // Reset auto-rotation timer
    if (autoRotate) {
      stopAutoRotation();
      // Small delay to prevent rapid restarts
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (autoRotate && !isAnimating) {
          startAutoRotation();
        }
      }, 100);
    }
  }

  function animateSlideTransition(fromIndex, toIndex) {
    const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-banner-slider__slide');
    
    if (fromIndex < 0 || fromIndex >= slides.length || toIndex < 0 || toIndex >= slides.length) {
      return;
    }
    
    // Set animation lock
    isAnimating = true;
    // console.log('🔒 Animation locked');
    
    const oldSlide = slides[fromIndex];
    const newSlide = slides[toIndex];
    
    // console.log(`=== ANIMATE TRANSITION ${fromIndex} → ${toIndex} ===`);
    
    // Step 1: Position new slide off-screen to the right
    newSlide.classList.remove('active', 'exiting-to-left');
    newSlide.classList.add('entering-from-right');
    
    // Force reflow
    newSlide.offsetHeight;
    
    // Step 2: Start animation - new slide enters, old slide exits
    setTimeout(() => {
      // New slide becomes active (enters from right)
      newSlide.classList.remove('entering-from-right');
      newSlide.classList.add('active');
      
      // Old slide exits to left
      oldSlide.classList.remove('active');
      oldSlide.classList.add('exiting-to-left');
      
      // console.log(`Old slide ${fromIndex}: exiting-to-left`);
      // console.log(`New slide ${toIndex}: active`);
    }, 10);
    
    // Step 3: Clean up after animation (without visible transition)
    setTimeout(() => {
      // Temporarily disable transitions for cleanup
      oldSlide.style.transition = 'none';
      
      // Position old slide back to right for future use
      oldSlide.classList.remove('exiting-to-left');
      oldSlide.classList.add('entering-from-right');
      
      // Force reflow to ensure the position change happens without transition
      oldSlide.offsetHeight;
      
      // Re-enable transitions for future animations
      oldSlide.style.transition = '';
      
      // console.log(`Cleanup: slide ${fromIndex} reset to entering-from-right (no transition)`);
      
      // Release animation lock
      isAnimating = false;
      // console.log('🔓 Animation unlocked');
    }, 650); // After 0.6s animation + buffer
  }

  function updateDots() {
    const dots = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-banner-slider__dot');
    dots.forEach((dot, index) => {
      dot.classList.toggle('active', index === currentSlide);
    });
  }



  function startAutoRotation() {
    if (!autoRotate) return;
    
    // Always clear any existing interval first
    stopAutoRotation();
    
    slideInterval = setInterval(() => {
      changeSlide(1);
    }, slideChangeInterval);
    
    // console.log('🔄 Auto-rotation started with interval:', slideChangeInterval + 'ms');
  }

  function stopAutoRotation() {
    if (slideInterval) {
      clearInterval(slideInterval);
      slideInterval = null;
      // console.log('⏹️ Auto-rotation stopped');
    }
  }

  // Initialize slider when DOM is loaded
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initSlider);
      } else {
    // DOM is already ready
    setTimeout(initSlider, 100);
  }

  // Handle keyboard navigation
  document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft') {
      changeSlide(-1);
    } else if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') {
      changeSlide(1);
    }
  });
</script>



</div></div>

					(function () {
						function changePosition() {
							if (window.innerWidth < 1100) return;

							const mediaElement = document.querySelector(
								`#shopify-section-template--25716136444088__popular-products .swiper .product-card .media img, #shopify-section-template--25716136444088__popular-products .swiper .product-card .media svg`
							);

							if (mediaElement) {
								const height = mediaElement.getBoundingClientRect().height;
								document
									.querySelectorAll(`#shopify-section-template--25716136444088__popular-products .swiper-button`)
									.forEach((button) => {
										button.style.top = height / 2 + 'px';
									});
							}
						}

						setTimeout(() => {
							changePosition();
						}, 200);
						document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', function () {
							setTimeout(() => {
								changePosition();
							}, 200);
						});
						window.addEventListener('resize', function () {
							setTimeout(() => {
								changePosition();
							}, 200);
						});
					})();
				</script>
